ethernet sla
 profile SLA1_LOSS type cfm-synthetic-loss-measurement
  probe
   send burst every 60 seconds packet count 60 interval 1 seconds
   priority 1
  !
  schedule
   every 1 minutes for 1 minutes
  !
  statistics
   measure one-way-loss-sd
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 5
   !
   measure one-way-loss-ds
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 5
   !
  !
 !
 profile SLA2_ROUNDTRIP type cfm-delay-measurement
  probe
   send burst every 60 seconds packet count 60 interval 1 seconds
   priority 1
  !
  schedule
   every 1 minutes for 1 minutes
  !
  statistics
   measure round-trip-delay
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 2
   !
   measure round-trip-jitter
    buckets size 1 probes
    buckets archive 2
   !
  !
 !

!
community-set OSPF100toEBGP
  500:500
end-set
!
community-set BGPLU_COMM_UNIP_MBH
  #UNIP
  100:100
end-set
!
route-policy BGP2UNIP
  if as-path in (ios-regex '^65112') then
    drop
  elseif community matches-any OSPF100toEBGP then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DENY_ALL
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy FIB-DROP
  # Route-policy to exclude SHT and SNW IPRAN prefixes
  if destination in FIB-DROP-SHT-PREFIXES or destination in FIB-DROP-SNW-PREFIXES then
    pass
  else
    # Route-policy to prevent selected IPCORE and IPRAN prefixes into FIB due to CSCvr41333
    if destination in FIB-DROP-PREFIXES then
      drop
    else
      pass
    endif
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VCORE_IN
  if ((extcommunity rt matches-any VCORE-Import_RT) and (destination in PFX_VCORE_IN)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any (65535:61102) and (destination in PFX_VCORE_Gy_mvno_IN)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any (65535:61221) and (destination in PFX_VCORE_Gx_IN)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any (65535:66502) and (destination in DCFW_Core_InterVDOM_Pfx01)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any (65535:66504) and (destination in DCFW-Prod-InterVDOM-Pfx01)) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy pass-all
  pass
end-policy
!
route-policy VAS_EXT_IN
  if ((extcommunity rt matches-any VAS_EXT_RT) and (destination in PFX_VAS_EXT_IN)) then
    pass
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any VAS_EXT_RT00)) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DHCP_IN_RPL
  if ((extcommunity rt matches-any DHCP_filter_VOBB_EXT) and (destination in DHCP_IN)) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VAS_PROD_IN

  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any NGIN_SIGTRAN-Ex-RT) and (destination in pfx_NGIN_SIGTRAN-Import-RT1_permit)) then

    pass

    pass
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any Gy_mvno-CBS) and (destination in pfx_Gy_mvno-CBS)) then
    pass
  elseif ((extcommunity rt matches-any SD_TxNMS-Imp-RT) and (destination in TxNMS-Import-Pfx1)) then
    pass
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any 98) then
    drop
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any NGIN_SIGTRAN-Ex-RT) then
    drop
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any TWAMP-RT) then
    drop
  elseif (extcommunity rt matches-any SD_NB-Ex-RT) then

    pass
  endif
end-policy
